(defn <-pgobject
  "Transform PGobject containing `json` or `jsonb` value to Clojure
  data."
  [^org.postgresql.util.PGobject v]
  (let [type  (.getType v)
        value (.getValue v)]
    (if (#{"jsonb" "json"} type)
      (when value

        (println ">> ===============================================")
        (println ">>1a " value)
        (println ">>1d " type)
        (println ">>1b " (class value))
        (println ">>1c " (<-json value))
        (println ">>1d " (class (<-json value)))
        (println ">> ===============================================")

        ;(let [converted-value (convert-string-to-symbol value)]
        ;  (with-meta converted-value {:pgtype type})))

        (with-meta (<-json value) {:pgtype type}))      ;; FIXME: before
        ;(<-json value)) ;; works
      value)))
